Page 6

Current Affairs Commentary

Gandhi's Non-Violent Resistance in India 13

Gandhi's non-violent resistance in India, breaking the salt law, is already underway. Regardless of whether it succeeds in the future, his actions of not seeking personal gain, not sacrificing others and acting as an example himself, fearing hardship, and not avoiding danger, are pure and sincere, and are truly seen and heard by the world. It is neither seeking private interests, nor privately avenging private hatreds. Harm falls first on oneself, and benefit extends to all people. This is truly rare and commendable.

People can prepare to lose money in order to trade for profit. People can prepare to sacrifice their own lives in order to fight with others. People can prepare to abandon all that they have in order to fight with others. Their doctrines may not be entirely correct, but their sincere intentions are known to others. It is not seeking luck, it is not speculation, it is not taking advantage of it for profit. It is clear to everyone. If one does not deeply understand that it is necessary to do so, and is forced to do so, then one will never do so.

A good deed that causes no loss to oneself can be done by everyone. A good deed that causes no loss to oneself and even brings benefits is something that everyone is happy to do. However, the good deeds of the world cannot be done so easily. Moreover, when seeking a right or recovering a benefit from the public, it is under strong pressure. Even seeking great gains with small sacrifices is still impossible. How can one act in a way that seeks luck and speculation in order to profit from it? Therefore, looking at Gandhi's non-violent resistance, he shoulders the burden and does not take shortcuts or seek profit. This can serve as an example for those who fight for the public.

Negotiations on International Telecommunications 18

(Nanjing) The International Telecommunications Negotiation Committee of the Ministry of Communications held its first meeting with the Pacific Commercial Cable Company on the afternoon of the 7th. The committee members from the Ministry of Communications were Zhuang Zhihuan and four others. The company was represented by Tao Te, as Deputy Manager Di Gengji was still unwell. Zhuang Zhihuan delivered a speech, stating that the company completed the Pacific cable connecting the United States and China in 1904 and has been handling telecommunications with the Chinese Telegraph Administration for nearly 30 years. Now, due to changes in China's political and economic situation and its relationship with international telecommunications, the telecommunications contracts previously signed with the company and Great Northern Telegraph Company and Eastern Extension Australasia and China Telegraph Company are no longer applicable. In the future, international telecommunications should be developed in accordance with the Chinese Kuomintang's party platform, the Premier's teachings, and the spirit of Chinese national independence. Sino-American relations are traditionally strong and the distance between them is vast. Telecommunications

should be vigorously promoted to bring the governments and people of the two countries closer and more friendly. Therefore, it is hoped that the company will sympathize with the new telegram transmission methods to be agreed upon. This meeting will first discuss and determine the outline, then discuss the details, and achieve satisfactory results in the shortest possible time. Tao Te then replied, stating that the company's cable has been communicating with China for more than 20 years and is truly the only tool for transmitting news between the United States and China. He hoped that both parties would cooperate sincerely to achieve satisfactory results. They then exchanged views and adjourned. (7th Special Dispatch)

Relief Grain Cannot Be Transported to Shaanxi 19

The Relief Association Opposes Monetization

(Beiping) The Beiping Shaanxi Relief Association requested the China International Famine Relief Commission to monetize the relief grain because it could not be transported to Shaanxi and remit the cash to Shaanxi for officials to distribute. The China International Famine Relief Commission discussed this today and did not agree, stating that there are no military affairs between Beiping and Shaanxi. If there is sincerity in assisting relief, only two or three rows of covered wagons are needed to distribute it. If the grain is monetized, there will be losses in price, and there is no guarantee that the cash will benefit the disaster victims when it arrives in Shaanxi. Therefore, they replied, requesting that wagons still be prepared to send grain to Shaanxi. (7th Special Dispatch)

Land Law Drafting Completed 29

(Nanjing) The Land Law Drafting Committee of the Legislative Yuan has completed drafting the Land Law, which is divided into five parts: 1. Land Law, 2. Land Registration Law, 3. Land Use Law, 4. Land Price Law, and 5. Land Expropriation Law. The entire text is based on the 14th item of the Kuomintang's political platform. The review has begun at the Legislative Yuan in recent days. The President of the Yuan, Hu Hanmin, and the President of the Judicial Yuan, Wang Chonghui, both attend the meeting every day. Currently, the first and second parts, except for one or two issues that have been reserved, have been reviewed. The government will continue to review the remaining parts from Tuesday to Friday. (7th Special Dispatch)

Constitution, 3. Civil Law and Commercial Law, 4. Criminal Law, 5. Civil Procedure Law, 6. Criminal Procedure Law, 7. Court Organization Law, 8. Administrative Law, 9. Public International Law, 10. Private International Law, 11. Political Science, 12. Economics, 13. Sociology, 14. Labor Law. International News

The Naval Conference Enters Liquidation Phase

Britain, the United States, and Japan Now Have a Concrete Agreement

There Is Still Hope for a Five-Power Agreement

Tokyo, July 7th, Japanese United Press - A telegram from London on the 6th stated that the naval disarmament conference has entered the liquidation phase this week and is scheduled to discuss the flexible issue of submarines at a special committee meeting on the afternoon of the 8th. However, it seems that Britain and the United States are unwilling to easily agree

to flexibility, or it is said that they are unwilling to recognize even 10% of flexibility. However, there seems to be hope for an agreement on the construction of light cruisers and destroyers. The issue of retaining Japan's freedom to build large cruisers is also relatively easy to resolve. Therefore, Britain, the United States, and Japan will draft a treaty within this period. If France and Italy withdraw from the conference, it can be closed before Easter.

London, July 6th, Reuters - U.S. Representative Gibson sent a radio telegram to the U.S. reporting on the progress of the Naval Conference, stating that Britain, the United States, and Japan have reached a concrete agreement in the past week. The three countries' fleets will jointly dismantle nine battleships without replenishment. According to this method, the Japanese fleet will have nine battleships. Therefore, the battleships dismantled by the three countries' fleets are numerically equal to the third largest battleship fleet in the world. Furthermore, according to last week's agreement, no battleships will be built in the next six years. The Naval Conference also agreed to limit the basis for various warships of the three countries. Therefore, the tonnage of cruisers, destroyers, and submarines of the three countries will be lower than the minimum limit discussed in Geneva in 1927. As for the current discussions between Britain, France, and Italy, there is still hope for a five-power agreement.

London, July 6th, Reuters - French Foreign Minister Briand returned to Paris last night to report everything to the government and is expected to return around Tuesday. London has no important announcements for the time being. There will be nine questions in the House of Commons tomorrow, all related to the political issues of the Naval Conference and Article 16 of the League of Nations Charter, fearing that the formula for interpreting the article contains the meaning of a guarantee to France. However, the Prime Minister has repeatedly stated that the British government is willing to determine the extent of British obligations, but is not prepared to increase its burden. The Observer reported that if a far-reaching disarmament agreement is to be reached, France is indispensable. If the existing obligations in the League of Nations Charter or the Locarno Agreement with Germany can be reaffirmed to satisfy France and accommodate the scope of disarmament, it is the responsibility of British diplomats to find a way to achieve it. The British delegation's opinion is probably like this.

Rome, July 6th, National Press - Italian newspapers commented on the Five-Power Naval Conference, mostly believing that a breakdown is imminent and repeatedly claiming that Italy will never accept a formula that is flexible and ambiguous, which France strongly desires to be approved at the meeting. As the Italian Kirang News said, Italy will never abandon its demand to be a naval power equal to France, and will not yield even under pressure. Even if this conference ends without results, the responsibility for its failure should not be borne by Italy. The Forum News also said that the only achievement of this Naval Conference is to accurately show that the countries that formerly fought together cannot reach an agreement. Paris, July 6th, National Press - Briand returned to Paris from London yesterday and will return to London on Tuesday to make a final effort to avoid the breakdown of the conference. However, at present, newspapers and political circles are increasingly impatient with the Naval Conference and no longer have any hope of success. Only officialdom still believes that a way can be found to preserve the face of the five powers and prevent them from separating.

New York, July 5th, National Press - U.S. Ambassador to Belgium Gibson gave a speech on the radio station in London today and was broadcast to the whole country by various radio stations in the United States. He said that there are good reasons to hope that a five-power agreement can be signed before we leave London. This can be known within these few days.

Use of Surplus Funds After Japanese Disarmament 45

Military Authorities Plan to Expand Air Force Strength

Tokyo, July 7th, Electric Communications Agency - The government is paying attention to how much of the surplus funds from disarmament will be used to reduce the burden on the people, that is, tax cuts and other social policies. The navy believes that there are many points of dissatisfaction in national defense in this agreement and intends to request new funding to strengthen naval power to compensate. The government and the party intend to recognize the navy's request to a considerable extent, but most of it is still intended to be used for tax cuts and social policies to fulfill its commitment to the people. Therefore, although the three-country agreement can be successful, there are still problems in domestic politics. The Seiyukai said that although the disarmament agreement can be established, this agreement was established in disregard of the military's opposition. It seems that huge expenses are required to strengthen the naval power outside the agreement. It is doubtful whether it can be used for tax cuts. Currently, the agreement on maintaining shipbuilding power has not yet been established. Therefore, the amount of surplus financial resources cannot be determined. If the navy's request is fully accommodated, then the tax cut is completely hopeless. Therefore, this disarmament is still equal to zero. Therefore, when compiling the budget, it is necessary to cut the navy's request or find new financial resources. However, the Ministry of Finance hopes to use 20 million yuan for tax cuts. If it is only this amount, it may not be difficult. Tokyo, July 7th, Japanese United Press - Today, the newspapers here published their editorials, discussing the use of the shipbuilding fees saved after the establishment of the disarmament agreement, and all opposed the navy's idea of diverting them to aviation maintenance, advocating that they be used to reduce the burden on the people.

Tokyo, July 7th, Japanese United Press - During this military and political reform, the Army Department plans to expand the Hang Kong Force. In recent days, it has sent members of the Military and Political Investigation Committee to inspect various flying teams and flying schools to study the methods of changing their content. In the future, each army must have at least one unit, but the cost is very high, with each heavy bomber costing 200,000 yuan and each light bomber costing 60,000 to 70,000 yuan. The Ministry of Military Affairs plans to sacrifice other types of aircraft teams and schools to seek the expansion of the bomber unit.

Tokyo, July 7th, Electric Communications Agency - The General Staff believes that according to this agreement, the strength of the three-country treaty cannot completely maintain national defense, and intends to draft a new expansion plan. The Navy Province refers to the plan of the General Staff. In order to compensate for the lack of submarine strength, it intends to greatly expand the air force, continue for five years, and request construction fees of 150 million yuan and maintenance fees of 100 million yuan by the eleventh year, totaling 250 million yuan. In order to compensate for the failure to implement the 70% requirement for large cruisers, it intends to request special expenses, such as modification fees, repair fees, exercise fees, and fuel fees. After the overall agreement is reached, it will submit a concrete plan.

People's Salt Is Sometimes Confiscated

Ellorkat, July 6th, Reuters - Non-violent resisters made salt on the shores of Salt Lake today, and many people came to watch. However, they were blocked by the police half a mile from the lake. The salt makers gave salt to the reporters at the scene. The Reuters reporter also got a little salt. This salt has not been refined and looks like sand, but it tastes salty. In the evening, some people sold refined salt made by the people in Kalkat. The price was surprisingly high. What usually sells for one rupee was sold for twenty-five rupees. Although this refined salt can be regarded as a commodity, it is still questionable whether it is absolutely edible. Page 8

One ton of salt obtained by 150 volunteers in Baduri and Jalalpur. Volunteers three miles from Dandi are now starting to collect salt again.

US Commemoration of Declaration of War Against Germany 50

National News Agency, Washington, 6th - Thirteen years ago today marked the date of the US declaration of war against Germany. Currently, the major powers are working together in London to eliminate the scourge of war, but progress is slow, and the outcome remains uncertain. Today, the world has more than six million people under arms in 58 countries. Naval competition, except for battleships, remains unrestricted. The Five-Power Naval Treaty is gradually fading into oblivion within these few days. A Three-Power agreement may be established, and the Atlantic and Pacific regions may be temporarily calm, but in the Mediterranean region, unless the differences between Italy and France can be reconciled, the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan will have no significant ability to influence the situation. Today, the entire United States is commemorating the day, and troops in various locations are conducting drills. Special prayers are also being held in classrooms.

The House of Representatives will hold elections for the chairmen of the plenary committees and standing committees, and will also elect the chairmen of the standing committees. The House of Peers will also elect the chairman of the plenary committee and the members of the standing committees. April 25th, Prime Minister Hamaguchi will deliver a policy speech in both houses, but if the negotiating committees of the various factions decide that the plenary sessions will be held every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday, then the Prime Minister's speech will be postponed to April 26th.

Important News

Sino-Czech Commercial Treaty Announced 58

The Sino-Czechoslovakian Treaty of Commerce and Friendship signed by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Czechoslovakian representative was officially announced by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs today (7th). The full text is as follows:

"The Great Republic of China and the Great Czechoslovak Republic, in order to establish"

Friendly relations between the two countries and facilitate trade between their peoples, have decided to conclude a Treaty of Friendship and Commerce based on the principles of equality and mutual respect for sovereignty. To this end, they have appointed as their plenipotentiaries: the Chairman of the National Government of the Great Republic of China, Wang Zhengting, Minister of Foreign Affairs of the National Government of the Great Republic of China, and the President of the Great Czechoslovak Republic, Ni Tzu-tou, Plenipotentiary of the Great Czechoslovak Republic. The two plenipotentiaries, having exchanged their full powers, found to be in good and due form, have agreed upon the following articles: (Article 1) There shall be perpetual peace and friendship between the Great Republic of China and the Great Czechoslovak Republic and their peoples. (Article 2) Each of the High Contracting Parties shall have the right to send duly accredited diplomatic representatives to the other. Such representatives shall enjoy in the country to which they are accredited all the rights, privileges, and immunities generally recognized by public international law. (Article 3) Each of the High Contracting Parties may appoint consuls-general, consuls, vice-consuls, and consular agents to reside in the territories of the other in such places as may be agreed upon. Such consular officers shall enjoy such treatment as is usually extended to consular officers of their rank. Before entering upon their duties, such consular officers shall, in accordance with international practice, obtain from the government of the country in which they are to serve an exequatur which may be withdrawn by the said government. Neither Government shall appoint persons engaged in trade or commerce as consular officers, other than honorary consuls. (Article 4) The nationals of each of the High Contracting Parties shall be free to enter or leave the territories of the other, provided that they are in possession of passports duly issued by their competent authorities and establishing their nationality. Such passports must be visé by the competent authorities of the country to which they proceed. (Article 5) The nationals of each of the High Contracting Parties shall receive in the territories of the other full protection for their persons and property in conformity with the laws and regulations of the country. They shall be permitted to travel, reside, establish themselves, and engage in trade or industry, and to acquire or lease property, subject always to the limitations which are or may be applicable to all aliens alike. They shall, in all that relates thereto, be subject to the laws, regulations, and jurisdictions of the country wherein they reside. (Article 6) The nationals of each of the High Contracting Parties shall be subject to the laws and regulations and to the jurisdiction of the courts of the country in which they reside. The nationals of each of the High Contracting Parties shall have the right to sue and be sued in the courts of the other and shall have free choice of advocates and representatives. They shall be entitled, in any case when the presence of an interpreter is considered by the court as necessary, to summon such an interpreter. (Article 7) The nationals of each of the High Contracting Parties in the territories of the other shall be required to pay the taxes prescribed by the laws and regulations of the country, but such taxes shall not be other or higher than those which are paid by the nationals of the country. (Article 8) Male and female workers of each of the High Contracting Parties shall enjoy the facility to enter into the territory of the other and shall, according to the laws and regulations of the country applicable to all foreign workers, enjoy the same treatment and protection as the national workers of the country. (Article 9) The nationals of each of the High Contracting Parties shall be exempt in the territories of the other from all compulsory military service whatsoever in the army, navy, air force, national defense force, or militia, as well as from all contributions imposed in lieu of personal service, and from all forced loans or military exactions or contributions. (Article 10) The Governments of the High Contracting Parties shall not subject the persons or houses of the nationals of each other to search without a warrant duly issued in accordance with the law in force. (Article 11) The nationals of each of the High Contracting Parties shall have in the territories of the other the right to dispose freely of their personal and real property by will or otherwise in accordance with the laws of the country. Whenever a national of one of the High Contracting Parties dies in the territories of the other, the competent local authority shall at once inform the nearest consular officer of the country of the deceased. If such consular officer should be the first to receive the information of such death, he shall immediately notify the local authority. In all matters of inheritance the law of the country of which the deceased was a national shall be applied. In case such national possessed in the territories of the other personal or real property, such consular officer or his nominee, in collaboration with the local authorities, shall administer such property in accordance with the laws of the country of the deceased. In case there is no heir or testamentary executor according to the laws of the country of the deceased, the property shall be dealt with according to the laws of the country wherein the property is situated. Any dispute arising out of matters of inheritance in the country where the property is situated shall be decided by the courts of the latter country. Whenever a national of one of the High Contracting Parties dies at sea or dies in the territories of the other Party without having a fixed domicile or permanent residence but while passing through such territory, his personal effects and valuables shall be delivered without any formality to the nearest consular officer of the country of the deceased for further handling. In all cases concerning inheritance the nationals of either High Contracting Party shall not be subjected in the territories of the other Party to taxes other or higher than those paid by the nationals of that Party in similar cases. (Article 12) The High Contracting Parties agree that customs duties and all related matters shall be entirely regulated by the domestic legislation of each country. The High Contracting Parties further agree that the nationals of each of the High Contracting Parties shall enjoy in the territories of the other, in all that concerns customs duties and related matters, treatment not in any respect less favorable than that which is or may be accorded to nationals of any other country. Neither High Contracting Party shall, on any pretext whatsoever, impose on articles the produce or manufacture of the other Party, imported into, or exported from, its territories, any customs duties or internal charges or taxes of any kind whatever other or higher than those which are or may be imposed on the like articles being the produce or manufacture of any other foreign country. (Article 13) Neither of the High Contracting Parties shall establish, in its own territory, prohibitions or restrictions of importation or exportation of goods produced or manufactured in either country, which shall not be applicable to the same goods when imported from or exported to any third country. Nevertheless the Governments of either High Contracting Party may, at any time, establish prohibitions or restrictions of importation or exportation for reasons of national defense,

food, public order, culture, antiquities, state monopoly, sanitation of humans, domestic animals, and plants, protection of the national economy, and maintenance of good morals. (Article 14) Goods produced or manufactured in the territories of either High Contracting Party shall, when they are conveyed in transit through the territories of the other Party, whether such transit is direct or whether the goods are unloaded, stored, or reloaded, be exempt from all transit duties. (Article 15) The nationals of either High Contracting Party shall not be entitled to enjoy in the territories of the other Party rights of navigation on rivers and along the coast, but this stipulation does not affect the clauses in the international agreements concerning international rivers. (Article 16)

The Government of China allows Czech merchant ships to enter and anchor in all coastal trading ports that have been opened. These merchant ships shall comply with the laws of the Chinese government and all regulations of the various trading ports. Chinese merchant ships shall enjoy the same treatment in Czech ports. (Article 17) The Governments of the High Contracting Parties agree to protect the trademarks and designs used by the nationals of each other, which have been approved for registration by the competent authorities of the country in accordance with its laws and regulations. Any counterfeiting or forgery shall be prohibited and punished according to law. (Article 18) The High Contracting Parties agree that all provisions of this Treaty relating to the rights and obligations of the nationals of each other shall apply equally to corporations of the other party recognized by the laws of either Party, except where such rights and obligations by their nature are applicable only to natural persons. (Article 19) This Treaty shall come into force on the fifteenth day after the exchange of ratifications and shall remain in force for a period of three years. Six months before the expiry of this term, either of the High Contracting Parties may give notice of revision or termination. If neither Party gives notice of revision or termination before the expiry of that term, the Treaty shall continue in force, but either Party may at any time thereafter give notice of revision or termination, and the Treaty shall expire six months after the date of such notice. (Article 20) This Treaty shall be drawn up in triplicate in the Chinese, Czech, and English languages. In case of any divergence of interpretation, the English text shall prevail. (Article 1) This treaty shall be ratified by the two High Contracting Parties in accordance with statutory procedures within the shortest possible time. The instruments of ratification shall be exchanged in Nanjing. In witness whereof, the two plenipotentiaries have signed and sealed this treaty in duplicate, as a sign of good faith. Done at Nanjing this twelfth day of February, the nineteenth year of the Republic of China, corresponding to the twelfth day of February, one thousand nine hundred and thirty. [Signed] Wang Zhengting [Seal] Ni Tzu-tou [Seal]

64th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Executive Committee 59

At 3:00 PM on the 7th, the Central Executive Committee held its 64th Standing Committee Meeting. Attendees included Hu Hanmin, Chen Guofu, Sun Ke, and Tan Yankai. Attendees in a non-voting capacity included Fang Juehui, Zhou Qigang, Gu Yingfen, Ke Xing'e, Chen Zhaoying, Li Wenfan, Jiao Yitang, Zhu Peide, Chen Yaoyuan, Chen Lifu, Liu Luyin, Shao Lizi, Enke Batu, and Wang Chonghui. Chen Guofu chaired the meeting. Resolutions were as follows: (1) Passed measures to restrict party members from not attending revolutionary commemorative gatherings without due cause. (2) The Central Supervisory Committee's letter stating that Yan Xishan had launched military action and betrayed the Party and the country, and requesting that he be permanently expelled from the Party, was resolved to be carried out. (3) The Central Supervisory Committee sent five cases of disciplinary action against party members, including the permanent expulsion from the Party of Sun Guobao, (Suiyuan Division) Zhao Jingxuan, Meng Yunan, Wang Huafu (Zhangjiakou Municipal Executive Committee), Peng Qingrui, Fang Yongshan, Mei Jiyao, Luo Ruixiang (Hunan Linxiang), Peng Juxian (Hunan Yueyang), and nine others. Li Siping (Zhejiang Jiashan) was expelled from the Party for three years. All were resolved to be carried out.

Central and National Government Commemorative Week 60

Central Party Headquarters: At 9:00 AM on the 7th, the Central Party Headquarters held its 54th Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week in the Grand Auditorium. Approximately 500 people attended, including Central Committee members, staff from various departments and committees, and guests. After Chairman Sun Ke offered his respects, Liu Luyin reported that the Central Government had ordered a punitive expedition against Yan Xishan's rebellion. Before issuing the order, the Central Government adopted a lenient approach, using various peaceful methods to persuade and influence him, so that he would consider the suffering of the people and cooperate to complete the revolutionary cause. However, recently, peaceful methods have proven ineffective. The Central Government's painstaking efforts to achieve the peaceful unification goal in Sun Yat-sen's teachings have been

Excerpts from Important News, Part 2 61

Absolutely not accepting; treason becoming increasingly clear; remnants being recruited; fully entering a state of war; in past rebellions, such as the Gui clique rebellion, Feng Yuxiang's two rebellions, Tang Shengzhi's rebellion, and Shi Yousan's mutiny, none were not secretly instigated by Yan Xishan and used as a tool for disruption; their blatant actions have long been seen through by the central government; the reason for not immediately exposing them was simply to allow them to realize their errors on their own, to guide them towards good, and to maintain a peaceful situation; however, they still believe that the central government has not seen through their tricks, acting willfully without any scruples; how utterly foolish; Yan Xishan is accustomed to playing tricks, always using others as sacrifices; this time, even if someone is willing to be used by him again, he is determined not to directly bear the brunt himself; let us analyze the content of his rebellion; Yan, in order to hold the reins of the Northern Warlords, recognizes Feng Yuxiang as a formidable enemy, whose power must be overthrown; therefore, he incited Feng to rebel, when the first rebellion occurred, Yan ostensibly helped Feng, but actually helped the central government to hasten his defeat; he took the opportunity to incorporate his retreating troops to expand his own strength; subsequently, he deceived Feng into staging a second rebellion; when the central government forces reached Tongguan, he again wanted to seize the opportunity to eliminate the remnants of the Northwest Army, while simultaneously imprisoning Feng Yuxiang in Shanxi; this kind of conspiracy is deeply resented by many in the Northwest Army; this time, he is again letting Feng enter Shaanxi, assisting Feng in making trouble; Feng's troops do not believe that Yan's attempt can succeed, but are merely using this to extort military supplies and equipment, getting as much as they can; if one speaks of genuine alliance, no one can believe it; as for using the reorganized faction's disruptive methods, he believes that he has succeeded, but Chen Gongbo is essentially a speculator, seeking only profit; he has successively been a cat's paw for the Communist Party, Wang Jingwei, Li Zongren, and Tang Shengzhi, and each time he failed to get money; this time, he has hatched the same old scheme, but Yan is so cunning and shrewd, it is uncertain whether he will be deceived by Chen; now that the punitive order has been issued, military affairs are becoming increasingly tense; given the central government's strength and the precedents of suppressing rebellions in the past, it is believed that all counter-revolutionary factions can be quickly eliminated and completely wiped out; while one side uses force to suppress the existing rebellion, the other side should still use sincerity to influence and eliminate future rebellions; furthermore, peaceful construction methods should be used to consolidate the foundation of the party and the nation; as for the reasons why counter-revolutionary factions dare to rebel repeatedly, (1) it is because the people of the whole country have failed to jointly shoulder the responsibility of citizens, using genuine vision and great strength to clearly distinguish right from wrong, so that they have scruples and dare not recklessly defy what is right; (2) domestic public opinion has not been able to fully restrain and severely criticize all reactionary factions, causing the general public to still not recognize right from wrong, thereby weakening their concept of the nation; it is hoped that all comrades in the party will work hard to be responsible for propaganda, so that the reactionary faction will never rise again after it has fallen, and so on; the report was finished, and the meeting adjourned at 10:30.

The National Government held a memorial week for Sun Yat-sen at 10 a.m. on the same day; those present included Chiang Kai-shek, Tan Yankai, Wang Chonghui, Gu Yingfen, Soong Tzu-wen, Chu Pei-te, Chen Shaokuan, He Yaozu, Jin Handing, Yi Peiji, Liu Ruiheng, Zhang Nanxian, Yang Jie, etc., and more than 300 officials and military officers from the National Government; Chiang Kai-shek presided over the meeting; after the ceremony, Chiang made the following report:

"Fellow comrades, on Thursday, April 1, Yan Xishan assumed the false post of Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force of the Republic of China; Feng Yuxiang and Li Zongren also followed suit, assuming the false posts of Deputy Commander-in-Chief; this matter has already been published in various newspapers, and you must all know about it; although this matter seems significant, from the perspective of our revolutionary stance, it is not a big deal; they [Yan Xishan] are very afraid of the name of the National Revolution; not only warlords fear the word 'revolution,' but imperialists are also terrified of it; therefore, we are envied by many people; since starting from Guangdong, our revolutionary army has won every battle; they have seen that there is no way to deal with it, and they have no choice but to join the revolution; and we, due to environmental factors, have allowed them to mix in; now, their true colors as warlords can no longer be concealed, and are being exposed day by day; they do not want the people, do not want revolution, and are directly engaging in warlord behavior, letting the people see it; after we know this, on one hand, there is the National Revolutionary Army, and on the other hand, there are the warlord armies; we will see which one wins in the end; since Yan Xishan assumed the false post, his credibility with the revolution and the people has been completely lost, and he can no longer mix into the revolutionary ranks to carry out his traitorous activities; as for the issue of punishing Yan's rebellion, now all party departments and the general public advocate punishing Yan Xishan; however, in the opinion of the government, there is no need to use troops to punish him; although Yan Xishan's counter-revolutionary behavior has been exposed, his weaknesses are not yet fully apparent; they think this rebellion is a big deal, but we can treat it as a small matter, or even as if it never happened; I believe that in the near future, they themselves will punish themselves; not only will those they consider friendly forces clash with each other, but their subordinates will probably punish them as well; therefore, the government does not need to use troops for the time being; I may go to inspect the Jinpu and Pinghan Railways in a couple of days, but it is not to command troops to punish them; now, the most important thing for us is internal rectification; whether in military, political, or party affairs, we must all work hard ourselves; if we can do this, even without using troops, the reactionary factions will naturally be eliminated; if we do not work hard ourselves, even without reactionary factions, we will still be eliminated; therefore, now we should strive to rectify all aspects of society, politics, and economics; this time in Zhejiang, I saw that the shortcomings we had before, which were unsatisfactory to the general public and feared and envied by the reactionary factions, have not been corrected; there are also many young people who do not know how to achieve the goals of the revolution, and their expectations for the government are too high; the government can never completely accomplish the cause of the revolution in a day; also, I heard that party departments in the countryside do not allow people to visit graves or burn paper ashes; not allowing the burning of paper ashes is appropriate, and no one would encourage the burning of paper ashes; but they should know that there are more than 500,000 people engaged in the business of making paper ashes; if burning paper ashes is prohibited, at least 500,000 people will lose their jobs; it is easy for the government to issue an order, but if many people lose their jobs before a relief method is devised, can the government bear this responsibility? Otherwise, wouldn't it merely create unrest in society? Therefore, many young people are ignorant, and this is just one example; there are many other similar cases; also, the matter of sweeping tombs is a custom that has existed in our country for thousands of years; of course, the government has no order prohibiting it, but the lower-level party departments are ignorant, causing misunderstandings in society;

There was a labor strike at Jardine Matheson the day before yesterday, followed by a student parade; the education sector and the government must take responsibility for this; now the reactionary factions are spreading rumors, even saying that the British killed four Jardine Matheson workers; this is completely untrue; it must be understood that under a revolutionary government, our citizens will not be killed by foreigners without cause; the municipal government and the education department should inform the principals of all schools that if students lightly listen to rumors and become tools for the reactionary factions, and take excessive actions, the government will treat them as counter-revolutionaries; it must be understood that in the era of the counter-revolutionary government in Beijing, it was understandable for young people to feel moved by the revolution; now, under a revolutionary government, acting against the revolution is tantamount to cutting oneself off from the revolution, not only will one be punished, but one will also bear the title of counter-revolutionary, and there will be no leniency;

Therefore, now if any school or organization disobeys government orders and stirs up trouble without cause, the government will severely punish them; now that the reactionary factions are rising up day by day, it is precisely the time for us to work hard and struggle; in the past, Sun Yat-sen was able to consolidate the foundation of the revolution and develop the revolutionary forces in a very small place in Guangdong; now, the territory is much larger than before, and the economic and military strength are superior to what it was before; any reactionary faction can be eliminated; it is hoped that everyone will continue the revolutionary spirit of Sun Yat-sen, consolidate the foundation of the revolution, and not allow the revolutionary cause of Sun Yat-sen's decades to be destroyed by others; as long as we ourselves are sound and the interior is consolidated, no one can be our enemy; the more enemies there are, the brighter and more hopeful our revolutionary future will be; as long as we rectify the interior and work together to build, the reactionary warlords will be eliminated without the need for troops; I will be going out again in a day or two; I hope everyone will pay attention to rectifying the interior, especially the various agencies in the capital, to revitalize their spirits; we do not need to use troops to punish the rebels, sacrificing the lives of soldiers and the property of the people; we are very confident that we will soon be able to eliminate all the reactionary factions and the country will achieve genuine unification; this is what I offer to everyone today."

Jinan Declares Martial Law 62

Jinan Correspondence: The Shandong Provincial Government and the General Headquarters believe that Jinan is an important provincial capital, where people from all directions gather, and at this time of many troubles, it is not enough to maintain public order without officially declaring martial law; therefore, it is hereby announced today (the 5th) that martial law will be implemented throughout the city; Shi Zhongcheng, the Jinan Garrison Commander, and Li Yue, the Deputy Garrison Commander, are ordered to handle martial law matters; a separate martial law headquarters will not be established to unify authority; currently, in addition to the Provincial Government Guard Regiment and the Police Security Force, there are a total of no less than 20,000 troops stationed near the provincial capital; the defense is extremely solid; the martial law proclamation is recorded below: "This city is the important capital of the province, with transportation extending in all directions, and natives and sojourners reside here; petty thieves and treacherous individuals mix among them, taking advantage of opportunities to steal and provoke disturbances, which is detrimental to public order; now that the times are difficult, for the sake of order and tranquility, it is urgent to declare martial law to protect the people and pacify the community; all martial law matters are hereby assigned to Shi Zhongcheng, the Jinan Garrison Commander, and Li Cheng, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, is additionally appointed as Deputy Garrison Commander to handle all matters; all persons of all kinds are required to abide by the martial law regulations, maintain their livelihoods in peace, and not disturb each other, causing trouble for themselves; if there are lawless individuals who deliberately violate the prohibitions, they will be severely punished without leniency once discovered; attached martial law implementation regulations: (1) The urban area of Jinan is the martial law area; (2) The martial law time is from 12:00 noon to 5:00 a.m. the next morning, prohibiting pedestrians; (3) During martial law hours, no one is allowed to pass without a special pass; (4) During martial law hours, no gatherings, associations, strikes, market closures, or any collective activities of the masses are allowed; (5) No groups may obstruct military operations, and may be dissolved if necessary; (6) All entertainment venues must stop performing at 11:00 p.m. and may not exceed the time limit; (7) It is not allowed to privately carry firearms, ammunition, weapons, fire tools, or other dangerous items for military use; (8) It is not allowed to post propaganda slogans, pictures, words, or various printed materials without permission; (9) Suspicious postal letters and telegrams may be opened and inspected; (10) During the martial law period, buildings, pedestrians, vehicles, ships, and other items may be inspected with the permission of the highest officer, and traffic may be stopped if necessary; (11) Matters not covered by these martial law regulations shall be handled in accordance with martial law; (12) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation (April 5)."

Jinan Market and Finance Stagnant 63

Jinan Correspondence: In recent days, not only is the money market extremely tight in this port, but there is also a severe shortage of silver dollars and banknotes; silver shops dare not conduct transactions due to the lack of cash; therefore, although the Money Industry Association reported to the authorities yesterday, no transactions were made, and they did not even report today; since the silver industry has completely stagnated, all commercial activities are also affected; the most recent reason for this is that the Jinan branch of the Central Bank transported 400,000 silver dollars to Qingdao a few days ago, and the city suddenly felt a lack of silver dollars; also, due to the situation, the Central Bank completely withdrew all banknotes; the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications are also afraid of runs, affecting their business, so they are actively redeeming the banknotes they issued; the China Industrial Bank is also redeeming banknotes, withdrawing them but no longer issuing them; the amount of silver dollars in the market is gradually becoming scarce; however, most of the funds of the banks are loaned to various silver shops, and the silver shops then relend them to various local product merchants for business outside the city; the funds are not in Jinan; therefore, although the Bank of China has issued 3.6 million yuan in banknotes, the Bank of Communications has issued 3.1 million yuan, and the China Industrial Bank has issued 50,000 yuan, they are actively redeeming them, but very few are being recovered; knowing this situation, the banks are competing to urge the silver shops to repay their debts; the shops, with no funds on hand, cannot cope; they have been meeting for days to discuss solutions, first requesting the banks not to press for repayment for the time being; the banks refused; then, two methods were proposed: (1) repay the debts owed to the banks in Shanghai to avoid shaking Jinan's cash reserves; (2) ask the banks to transport silver dollars from various places to Jinan to circulate in the market and provide relief; however, it is not profitable to transport silver dollars to Jinan now, and due to the situation, the banks have not agreed to do so; in the past two days, cash is about 5 yuan more expensive per thousand yuan than deposits; it is extremely difficult to find 300 or 200 yuan in cash on the market; the shortage of cash is unprecedented in recent years (April 4-5).

Local Correspondence

Suzhou 64

Gunfire between Soldiers and Bandits at Da Yao Dang: In recent days, the large gangs of lake bandits in Yangcheng Lake, where the three counties of Wuxian, Kunshan, and Wujiang meet, have been attacked by the bandit suppression troops in Fan Tian, Chenmu's Sanyuan Dam, and other places between Weiting and Zhengyi; after the bandits were routed, they had no way to escape; around 2:00 p.m. on the 6th, more than 30 bandit ships sneaked into Chefang Township's Da Yao Dang; after reconnaissance, the Ninth Company Commander of the Second Battalion of the 25th Regiment of the Bandit Suppression Army, stationed in Chefang, led his troops to Da Yao; at 3:00 p.m., they opened fire on the lake bandits; the battle was fierce; unexpectedly, after the soldiers opened fire, more than 50 more bandit ships sailed from Yangcheng Lake to Da Yao, joining the large gang and resisting the government troops together; the battle lasted for five hours, sinking four bandit ships, killing and wounding 30 bandits, and capturing four bandits; the soldiers were injured when the bandits shot Leng, the second platoon leader of the Seventh Company, and 11 soldiers; Chief of Staff Liu immediately ordered the team to escort the wounded platoon leader and 11 others to Suzhou that night; they arrived in Suzhou yesterday (the 7th); six of them were sent to Shanghai for treatment, while platoon leader Leng and the other five were sent to the Gengsheng Hospital in Sibaidu for treatment; Commander Hu immediately went to the hospital to comfort them and rewarded the officer with 10 yuan and each soldier with 5 yuan to show encouragement; the four captured bandits were escorted to the Bandit Suppression Headquarters for punishment; at the same time, the Weiting garrison was notified to send a company of soldiers to transfer from Xietang to Da Yao to join the Seventh Company and continue to suppress the bandits; around 3:00 a.m. yesterday, the bandits were finally defeated and retreated in different directions; when the battle between the soldiers and bandits was fierce, the entire town of Chefang was extremely panicked; when the bandits retreated, the bandit suppression troops vigorously pursued and hunted them down, determined to wipe out the gang of lake bandits in one fell swoop;

Bandits Rob Security Corps Arms: Forty or so lake bandits suddenly arrived in Changxing's Guantai Township in Zhejiang and surrounded the town's Security Corps, carrying out a robbery; the Security Corps members were outnumbered and overwhelmed, and were eventually robbed of their rifles.

Jinshan 65

Teachers and Students Still Held in Bandit Lair: On the afternoon of the 1st, around 5:00 p.m., more than 30 bandit ships suddenly arrived in Zhangyan Town and carried out a massive robbery, as has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper; when the bandits left, they also kidnapped more than 60 hostages, and the teachers and students of Jinshan No. 2 Elementary School were the most numerous, totaling 34 people; of these, 18 poor teachers and students were released on the 2nd, and 16 are still held in the bandit lair; their names are listed below: Principal Wang Shichu, physical education teacher Zhang Zhaoying, students Zhao Weiting, Zhang Yejin, Huang Wenjun, Huang Gongsheng, Huang Quqing, Tao Guokang, Xi Chengyuan, Zhang Shouyi, Huang Weijing, Zhang Siming, Yao Shuping, Yao Xiuping, Wu Dongjun, Gu Shijie; according to someone released, the bandit lair is near the Dragon King Temple on the shores of Taihu Lake.

Wuxi 66

Lu Shiqiao Escorted to Suzhou for Trial: Lu Shiqiao, the former propaganda officer of the county party department in this county, was arrested on suspicion of shooting Tan Qixuan, the former director of the Beishang Township Administrative Bureau, and sentenced to one year and three months of imprisonment by the High Court, and returned to the original county for imprisonment; when Lu was detained in Suzhou, a prison riot occurred; the High Court has scheduled a hearing for the 8th of this month to pronounce the sentence; yesterday, County Magistrate Sun received an order from the High Court and immediately dispatched police to escort Lu to Suzhou to await trial.

Bandit Suppression Troops Advance to Suppress Bandits: The bandit suppression troops sent by the Central Government have defeated the bandits near Chenmu in Wu County and will soon be able to clear them out; Hu Zuyu, the commander-in-chief of bandit suppression, has recently issued a proclamation to the people of all counties along Taihu Lake, stating that those who can kill or capture bandits and their firearms will be rewarded; at the same time, he has also announced to the bandits that those who lead their troops to surrender, abandon the bandit gang, and reform themselves will be pardoned; Mao, the chief of the second district of the county's water police, received this proclamation yesterday and posted it everywhere to inform the public.

Changzhou 67

Confiscated Rice Boats Forced to Release: Qian Fengtai and other rice shops in Weicun Town, Wuyi County, were smuggling rice abroad when Zhang Hanqin, a patrol officer from the second outpost of the fourth branch of the Public Security Bureau in charge of the area, seized three rice boats and reported them to the County Government Public Security Bureau, which transferred the matter to the Civil Affairs Department for instructions on how to handle it; unexpectedly, when Patrol Officer Zhang came to the city on official business on the 2nd, the rice merchants pleaded with many people to force Guo Qinghai, the patrol leader in charge of guarding the rice boats, to release the rice boats; when Patrol Officer Zhang returned to the outpost and received a report of the previous events, he immediately reported it to the county bureau for investigation; Li Leng, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, was furious and immediately dispatched Zhao Bingheng, the captain of the Mauser squad, with eight soldiers to go to the countryside on the afternoon of the 6th to bring Patrol Leader Guo, who had released the rice boats without authorization, to the city for interrogation, and ordered Patrol Officer Zhang Hanqin to come to the city to inquire about everything.

Sailing Ship Robbed En Route: A sailing ship traveling from Wuxi to Jintan set off from Jintan on the morning of the 5th with more than 790 silver dollars in goods and money and returned to Wuxi; around 10:00 p.m. that night, when passing through the Haizhekou area in the western suburbs of Wuyi, four bandits suddenly jumped onto the ship, each armed with guns, and searched wantonly, taking more than 700 yuan from the silver box and more than 300 yuan hidden by the crew.

Nantong 68

Salt Yard Foreman Kidnapped: Xu Guoqing and other foremen of the Lvsi Tongrentai Salt Yard were kidnapped by sea bandits, and all the salt workers have ceased operations; Yuan Desheng, the director of the general yard in Tong County, reported this and urgently telegraphed the Nantong County Government for relief.

Landslides in Sanyu Town: A large band of bandits arrived in a town about seven miles from Sanyu Town on the 5th and robbed shops and residents; the military and police rushed to suppress them after hearing the news.

Rugao 69

Police Team Encircles and Suppresses the Er Yuan Gang: After the police from the Er Yuan and Shuangdun areas of the Da Gu bandits, who were entrenched in Er Yuan and Shuangdun, were jointly suppressed, they had fled far away; unexpectedly, as soon as the government troops returned to defense, the bandit flames reignited, and they suddenly carried out a large-scale burning and looting the other day, numbering about a thousand people; the two provincial police teams from Nantong were opened to Er Yuan, and the provincial police from Rugao also moved into Shuangdun, joining the district police team from Ma Jue, totaling about 500 people; they gathered at Er Yuan and launched a joint attack, encircling the bandits of about a thousand on all sides; the time for their elimination should not be far away.

Pinghu 70

Security Team Arrives in Pinghu to Increase Defense: Around 5:00 p.m. on the 6th, a company of soldiers (the fourth company of the first battalion of the seventh regiment of the provincial security team) arrived from Jiaxing; they stayed overnight at the Chenghuang Temple and set off for Xincang on the 7th to increase defense; Tugboat Sinks Steamer: The Xinjiaju steamer, which runs between Xiashi and Pinghu, outside the east gate of this city, was returning from Pinghu to Xia a few days ago when it passed through the Sigiao Bridge; due to the rapid currents in the bridge hole, the steamer was towing a boat fully loaded with people and goods; as soon as it left the bridge opening, it was violently hit by the towed boat, causing damage to the machinery and the sinking of the ship; fortunately, the people and goods were all on the towed boat and did not suffer major losses.

Shaoxing 71

Female Secretary Attempts Suicide and is Rescued: Li Zhenzhen, a female secretary of the county government, attempted suicide by taking medicine at the Dalu Xin Hotel on the afternoon of the 4th for unknown reasons; later, the tea boy discovered her lying stiffly on the bed; the hotel accountant reported it to the fifth outpost of the third branch, which reported it to the county government; County Magistrate Tang urgently telegraphed various doctors in the city to come to the hotel to provide medical assistance; fortunately, it was still early, and she was saved.

Shangyu 72

Robbery Occurs in Wan'ao: At about 11:00 p.m. on the night of the 3rd, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived at the homes of Ye Xinsheng and Ye Tianfu in Wan'ao Village, Dongxiang Township, broke down the doors and entered, first captured Ye Xinsheng, beat and kicked him, and threatened him to reveal where he had hidden his money; as a result, they robbed him of three or four hundred silver dollars and dozens of pieces of clothing; then they went to Ye Tianfu's home and used the same methods to rob him of thirty or forty silver dollars and twenty or thirty pieces of clothing; then they went towards Shipoqiao in Yuyao; the victim Ye Xinsheng's abdomen was kicked by the bandits and was seriously injured; Ye Tianfu was covered in bruises and swellings and was also seriously injured.

Funing 73

Bandits Clash with Police Team: Yesterday afternoon, more than a hundred bandits suddenly arrived in Qitao Town, Beixiang Township, in this county from Guanyun County; Huang Gongzheng, the captain of the police squadron stationed in the town, led his team to intercept them; the bandits resisted with gunfire, and a fierce battle lasted for several hours; Battalion Commander Xiong Yanghe was urgently informed and dispatched squad leaders Wang Buyun and Yu Yishou to lead their teams to rush to the scene overnight to assist in the suppression; five bandits were killed on the spot, and several were captured alive; the rest fled in different directions; it was reported that one police officer was also injured.

Since the opening of the National Games, the various sports have been enthusiastic and exceptional, and have aroused a very satisfactory audience and have progressively increased, with each venue being full during the duration of the conference, and the various businesses in Hangzhou have also greatly increased their business and profits, especially the transportation, hostels, food shops, and Hangzhou specialties, which have benefited the most, and automobiles have a busy and frenzied appearance, which yesterday was the seventh day of the conference. The ball games on this day were the secondary competition and there was a Weile group's performance. Chairman of the congress, Dai Jitao, vice chairman Zhang Jingjiang, He Jingzhi, preparation director Zhu Jiahua, deputy director Zhou Xiangxian and general manager Ma Xun, etc., were all in the arena to preside over everything, and Zhongwei Lin Musen, also came to Hangzhou to visit, and the swimming that began yesterday was held at the Zijiang University, and the highway bureau specially released a special car to carry athletes and staff, and the audience was also full of pits, since the opening of the conference, the grand situation was the most yesterday. Two Types of Performances 78

Yesterday, there were no competitions at the track and field stadium. Therefore, the Shanghai Weile Troupe performed a bicycle show, and the Hubei and Zhejiang Provinces National Martial Arts Hall performed martial arts. The Zhongshan Vocational School Party Boy Scouts participated in a gymnastics performance. Therefore, the spectators filled the seats by around 1 PM. The speed of the Chong Le Yuan bicycles was like lightning, leaving people in awe. The martial arts performance by Hubei National Martial Arts was as vigorous as a lively dragon and burning fire, having reached a state of perfect skill. Although the Zhejiang Province National Martial Arts Hall's public education training classes for youth, adults, and women had not been established for long, their achievements were already considerable. Yesterday's performances of Tan Legs, Xing Yi Quan, and Tai Chi Quan were like the first strokes of writing the Yellow Court Classic, perfectly executed, winning high praise from the audience.

China Advocates Using Old Rules for Far Eastern Games 79

The協進會 (Association) held a rules meeting last night and decided.

Amateur Qualifications to be Reviewed and Announced by Experts.

Special dispatch from Hangzhou this morning. Hao Boyang of the中華全國協進會 (All China Association), invited rules committee members Zhang Xinfu, Ma Yuehan, Gao Xiwei, Zhang Jiwu, Jiang Xiangqing, Hao Gengsheng, Xu Minhui, Dong Shouyi, Shu Hong, Qiu Jixiang, etc., last night. Hao first reported the purpose of the meeting and nominated Zhang Jiwu as chairman and Hao Gengsheng as recorder. (1) Japan sent a letter requesting that the rules of this Far Eastern Games be changed to be the same as those of the International Association, and that women's basketball adopt the men's rules. It was decided that this session should still use the old rules, and the three-nation committee would discuss it in detail when the next conference is held in Japan. (2) Regarding amateur qualifications, it was decided that the協進會 (Association) would invite experts to form a committee to review and announce them.

Chinese Female Athletes Participate in Far Eastern Games 80

Selection Committee Established

Dispatch from Hangzhou this morning. The selection committee for Chinese female athletes for the 9th Far Eastern Games held its inaugural committee meeting last night. Attendees included Ms. Gao Zi, Huang Shufang, He Guanchu, and Yang Xiaorang. Hao Boyang of the協進會 (Association) reported the purpose of the association's organization and nominated Gao Zi as chairman. It was decided that the track and field events would include 100-meter, 200-meter, long jump, triple jump, and 4x400-meter relay, with the number of athletes yet to be determined. The ball games would include tennis and volleyball, with basketball undecided. If Japan could adopt women's rules, it would be included. In addition, the association's committee members and Hao Boyang, Qiu Jixiang, and Li Feiyun were appointed to observe the volleyball and basketball female athletes separately and select them at a scheduled meeting.

Shanghai Wins Right to Finals

Shanghai 5 vs. 0 Guangdong

Hao Chunde of Shanghai, first in the pentathlon, photo by Wang Kai

(1) Shanghai vs. Guangdong Match

The soccer skills of the Shanghai and Guangdong teams have long been known. Yesterday was the date of the conference semi-finals, and the two teams played at the soccer field. Those who came to watch reached four or five thousand, packing the stands tightly, almost to capacity. The two teams fought fiercely for ninety minutes. Initially, the Guangdong team was able to maintain, but they became increasingly unable to support as the battle continued. As a result, Shanghai overwhelmingly defeated Guangdong 5-0, winning the right to the soccer finals. The audience unanimously praised them.

Lineups of the two teams

Team: Ning, Jingjing, Pu, Hongsheng, Qiu, Jietian

Sea: Xian, Shansi, Shilin, Qiaojia, Yong, Yu

Shang: Zhou, Li, Jiang, Sun, Chen, Zhuang, Dai, Xi, Chen, Wang, Chen

Position: Goalkeeper, Left Back, Right Back, Left Back, Right Back, Left Forward, Right Forward, Left Wing, Right Wing

Inside, Inside, Front, Front, Inside, Inside

Defense: Left, Right, Center, Left, Right, Center, Left, Right, Right, Left

Team: Payne, Enkun, He, Kang, Sheng, Fan, Zhaomin, Yao, Tie

East: Jun, Hong, Bing, Qing, Xi, Jia, Zong, Jia, Guang, Wei

Guang: Chen, Qu, Huang, Liu, Hu, Xu, Long, Xu, Zhuang, Chen, Gao

The weather was clear yesterday, and from 2:30 PM, even more spectators flocked to the soccer field. The road outside the field was congested, and the ticket office was crowded with people pushing and shoving, eager to get in. Young students were especially numerous, all with a sense of excitement, wanting to see the athletes of both teams display their skills.

As the bell rang three times, the team members of both teams entered the field one after another. After warming up, they lined up against each other. Shanghai defended the north, and Guangdong occupied the south. Both sides moved quickly and performed excellently, charging forward like breaking through bamboo. The beauty of their passes made the audience cheer endlessly. Initially, the strength of the teams was difficult to distinguish, and the situation seemed very even. The Guangdong forwards were very brave, but their shooting skills were too weak, making it difficult to score. Shanghai was strong, but they had to put in all their efforts to achieve victory.

The battle between the two sides was very intense. Sometimes the Shanghai team attacked, and the Guangdong team counterattacked. The Shanghai team maintained their usual standard, and although star players Li Huitang and Chen Zhenhe did not play, their strength was not reduced. Chen Guangyao performed the best for the Guangdong team. The inside defense was also good, but they were often flustered and made mistakes.

Kicking from the Ground 84

A few minutes after the match, Guangdong's Chen Guangyao rushed towards the Shanghai team. Jiang Shan Jing returned the attack not far away. At this time, the Shanghai team's goal was empty. Li Ning, without regard for his own safety, kicked the ball from the ground, earning a lot of applause.

Alarming Waves 85

The Guangdong forwards ran quickly, which was evident to the audience. After ten minutes, Chen Guangyao broke through and went straight to the end line to cross the ball. Four forwards rushed over, creating an uneasy situation in front of the Shanghai team's goal. Fortunately, Xian Yan and Li Ning were able to defend effectively, preventing any ambush.

Strict Inner Defense 86

The Shanghai team was unable to attack, so they changed their strategy and used a five-way encirclement to attack. However, the Guangdong team's inner defense was strict, making it difficult to break through. The more fiercely the Shanghai team attacked, the more vigilant the Guangdong team became. At this time, the Shanghai team could only sigh in vain.

Penalty Kick 87

Twenty minutes later, the Shanghai team attacked even more fiercely. The Guangdong goalkeeper made many high saves. At this time, an inside defender was penalized for touching the ball with his hand, resulting in a penalty kick. Dai Linjing took the kick and scored, opening the scoring.

Speed is Essential 88

At the start of the second half, after a few minutes of back-and-forth action, Xi Qiaosheng received the ball and passed it to Dai Linjing. Dai kicked the ball high, and the Guangdong goalkeeper jumped to save it, but the ball went into the net.

The prize presented by Zhang Xueliang, photo by Wang Kai

Distant Shot 89

Soon after, Shanghai's Zhuang Shihong received the ball 30 yards from the goal and shot towards the enemy's goal. The Guangdong goalkeeper parried the ball not far away, and Xi Qiaosheng, waiting for an opportunity, kicked it in, scoring a goal. Then, Wang Yongji scored another goal with the help of Chen Jiaqiu.

The Audience Cheered 90

In the midst of the melee, Dai got the ball and passed it to Chen Jiaqiu. Chen passed it back to Dai, and Dai passed it back to Chen Buyu Tian. Chen intercepted the ball and dribbled it past a defender, advancing rapidly as if he were in an uninhabited area. At the same time, the crowd roared with cheers. Yu Tian became even more inspired, rushing to the edge of the goal and kicking the ball hard into the net.

No Second Chance 91

At this point, the Guangdong team roared, and all their ailments seemed to disappear. Chen Guangyao charged repeatedly, but unfortunately, he was unsuccessful. Soon after, the whistle blew, and the Shanghai team won 5-0.

(2) Nanjing vs. Liaoning Match 92

Nanjing's strength and courage were superior to the Liaoning team.

They won more easily. The Liaoning team resisted with all their might, but the forwards had several excellent opportunities but failed to score. Unfortunately, their left-wingers He Rongzhang and Liu Baojun were often able to penetrate deep into enemy territory, creating a panic situation, but because the opposing inside defense was too strong, they were unable to achieve success.

One Breath 93

As soon as the two sides started fighting, the Liaoning team launched a full-scale attack. Not long after the start of the game, Nanjing's right winger Jiang Zhihong broke into the siege with great momentum, but was blocked by the Liaoning team's defense and failed to succeed. About a quarter of an hour into the game, the Liaoning center back suddenly got the ball and went over the defender, passing it to Wu Ronghe. Wu forcibly charged forward, with Cai Sicheng covering him on the side. The two advanced side by side, making it difficult for anyone to stop them. When he got close to the ball, Wu Ronghe kicked it, and the ball went into the net from the left corner, opening the scoring. After that, the Liaoning team became more and more courageous. The forwards charged several times and performed very well. The Nanjing team did not want to show weakness and counterattacked strongly. After several passes, the right inside forward Ling Yuanyang shot in a goal to tie the score. The most dangerous moment for the Liaoning team was when the Nanjing team took advantage of the Liaoning team's full-scale attack. The right winger Jiang Zhihong made an excellent pass, and center forward Gu Yuanliang had a good opportunity to shoot from six or seven yards from the goal, but the ball went too far to the side, otherwise the Liaoning team would have no chance. At thirty minutes, Liaoning made another valiant effort. The right inside forward got the ball and shot hard at the goal. The ball hit the crossbar and bounced back. Although the ball did not go in, the goalkeeper was already very nervous. After a period of melee, Liaoning's Cai Sicheng broke through and attacked again, but failed. After that, the attack and defense of both sides gradually became equal, and the situation was very balanced. The result of the first half was a 1-1 tie.

Decline 94

At the start of the second half, the Nanjing team gained momentum. The Liaoning inside defense fought bravely, making it impossible for the other side to have a chance to shoot. After entering, the Liaoning team made a great effort and launched a fierce attack. They had two corner kick opportunities, but they were ineffective. Unexpectedly, while the Nanjing team was trying hard to resist, a long pass led to the Liaoning team's demise. The left winger Liu Zukan shot in a goal. Subsequently, Liaoning also shot in a goal, but it was ruled out for offside.

Exhaustion 95

Twenty minutes later, the Nanjing left winger, with the help of Ling Yang, shot in another goal. Soon after, Liaoning also kicked in a goal from the center forward. After entering, Nanjing adopted a more defensive posture, attacking as the opportunity arose. Until the end, there were no more gains. As a result, Nanjing won 3-2.

Aftermath of the Game 96

Seeing the failure of the game, many of the Liaoning players swarmed into the field, making a fierce appearance, wanting to hit the umpire. Fortunately, after many people persuaded them, the matter was settled. It has been found that such behavior has become commonplace for the team members in this conference, which is a pity for the conference and a stain on the team. It is hoped that the team leaders will correct this during normal training.

Shanghai vs. Liaoning Game

The Strength of the Two Teams is Equally Matched

But Shanghai Has a Better Grasp of Shooting

Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, the Shanghai men's team and the Liaoning team held the second game. Shanghai basketball has long been famous, and Liaoning is based on Feng Yong University, with most of the players being former Tianjin Rotary Club players, such as Xian Zhuanghuai, Wu Jiqing, Ma Yu, Hua, etc., who are all Tianjin experts, so their strength is also very impressive. In the first half, the Shanghai team was dominant, with a score of 34 to 15, Shanghai won. In the second half, the Liaoning team gave it their all and changed their tactics, resulting in 29 to 19, Liaoning won. The total result was 53 to 44, Shanghai won, obtaining the right to the semi-finals today. The details of the competition are recorded below.

Smooth Sailing 99

The game started in the first half, and the two sides fought fiercely. There was no record in the first three minutes. In the fourth minute, Shanghai's Liang Guoquan opened the scoring, scoring a goal. Not long after, Liaoning's inside defender Ma Yuhua also scored a goal, making it 2 to 2. After one minute, Huang Yunli and Wang Jinpeng each scored a goal, making the score 8 to 2. Seeing that Shanghai was unstoppable, the Liaoning team immediately announced a timeout and replaced Wu Jiqing with Ma Bingjun as center forward. But since then, Shanghai has been smooth sailing, and the score has continued to rise. The Liaoning team's shots seem to be inaccurate. Although their cooperation is very good, they lost too many opportunities to no avail. The first half ended with a score of 34 to 15.

Final Struggle 100

As the whistle blew, the second half began. The Shanghai team replaced He Tong with Wei Haiqing as center forward. The Liaoning team had the determination to fight to the death and fought very fiercely. They also changed their strategy, attacking from a distance and attacking from close range, which was always beneficial. In the first ten minutes, they created a record of 15 to 5, with a total score of 39 to 30, Shanghai won, with a difference of only nine points. So Shanghai announced a timeout, and He Tong entered the field for the second time. The Shanghai team seemed to regain its previous courage, and He Tong also scored several goals in a row. Finally, the score in the second half was 29 to 19, Liaoning won, and the total score was 53 to 44, Shanghai won. In terms of the strength of the two teams, there is little difference, but Shanghai seems to have a better grasp of the shots.

Women's Volleyball 103

Yesterday's Semifinal Results: Shanghai and Guangdong Secure Spots in Finals

Championship Outcome to Be Decided Tomorrow

Guangdong Defeats Beiping A...Two Sets to Zero

Guangdong Team Excels in Offense and Defense

Beiping Team Lacks Coordination

After Guangdong and Beiping A Team Two successively defeated Shanghai B and Liaoning on the 4th, each obtained a semifinal qualification. At 1 PM on the 7th, the two teams competed in the volleyball court. The Guangdong team's players were well-rounded, with excellent coordination among the front, middle, and back rows. The Beiping lineup was also quite strong, but they lacked experience, and the initial formation was scattered. In the second set, they displayed a surprising performance, not discouraged by the loss, and their spirit was commendable. A brief account of the match follows:

At 1 PM, the female players from the North and South gracefully entered the court. Both teams were full of spirit and dressed neatly, especially the Guangdong team in white shirts and shorts, all with bare legs, resembling young boys, and their lively demeanor and exquisite posture indicated they were skilled players. As the game began, both teams vigorously attacked, but the Beiping formation was disorganized, with many mistakes. Guangdong, on the other hand, had a smooth start, scoring fourteen consecutive points. As a result, the Beiping team's morale was further shaken. Despite repeated efforts to compete, the score difference was too large to overcome. However, the situation gradually evened out, with progress on both sides. Before long, Guangdong won the first set 21-6.

Page 12

Starting with the second set, Beiping aimed to counterattack, with a very strong sense of unity. The front row's offense was quite effective, and the scores remained close. Although Guangdong initially took the lead at 11-9, Beiping made even greater efforts after that, engaging in a fierce battle for a long time, with the score suddenly increasing to 17-14, turning defeat into victory. Seeing the enemy's momentum, Guangdong also agreed to work together to cope, and their offensive and defensive methods were very appropriate. The performance at this time was very exciting, a sudden highlight compared to the previous sets. The outcome of each ball often involved ten or eight exchanges, with blocking and spiking, each team displaying its skills. One could only see hands weaving and palms extending above the net, with the ball rolling back and forth, making for a spectacular sight. Sometimes, even if the ball was hit out of the court, they could still use long-range passing to escape danger. The audience applauded and cheered loudly. In an instant, Beiping was still leading at 18-14. Then, Guangdong scored on a serve, resulting in a 19-19 tie. Subsequently, each team scored 20. At this critical juncture, the competition became even more intense, as the opportunity was fleeting, not allowing for the slightest delay. In the end, Guangdong gained the lead with a successful serve, winning two more points to win. Winning two consecutive sets, they secured the right to the final.

Judging from the teams' talent in today's match, Guangdong was more well-rounded. Beiping had many good players, but the skills of one or two were slightly weaker, resulting in a lack of coordination. Peng Jingbo in the middle row made the most mistakes. If this player had made greater efforts in the second set, they could have taken the lead earlier, and the outcome of the third set would have been uncertain. From this, it can be seen that the excellence of a team does not rely on a few exceptional talents, but rather on the effectiveness of coordination. Referee: Xu Minhui. The Zhijiang pool water is taken from mountain streams and springs, which are slightly cold. Yesterday, tin pipes were used to fill it with hot water, and the temperature was suitable for the athletes. After the swimmers first tried swimming, the competition began.

The mountains are green and lush, the pool water is blue-green, the waves are snow-white, and the sunshine is soft. The scenery is excellent. Standing on a high mountain and looking down is truly a spectacle.
